- ★ VEHICLE MOTION QUALITY ROUND 2 (2026-06-10): user clarified the complaint = CAR MOVEMENT choppiness, distinct from framerate. Found 3 sync-side defects independent of FPS: (1) dead-reckoning velocity was measured from CLIENT ARRIVAL times (frame-quantized ~90ms; sometimes 2 packets/frame) → velocity estimate jittered though the car moved steadily; (2) BUG: two packets in one frame hit the dt-guard and set Velocity=ZERO → extrapolation froze until next packet = stutter; (3) blend factor saturated (dt×14>1) at low FPS → every packet correction landed as an instant pop. (rule)
- FIX (deployed 2026-06-10, build clean): sender-clock timestamps added to the 3 motion payloads — TrafficSnapshotPayload.T, VehicleFleetPayload.T, PlayerPositionPayload.T (sender Time.unscaledTime at sample; receivers use DIFFS of the same sender''s stamps, so cross-machine clock offset is irrelevant). Receivers (TrafficGhost.HostT, RemoteVehicle.SenderT, RemotePlayerMover.SenderT) compute velocity from stamp deltas; tiny delta (<5ms) → KEEP previous velocity (never zero); blend k capped at 0.5 in all three movers so corrections spread ≥2 frames. RemotePlayerMover.SetTarget now takes senderT. BOTH SIDES MUST RUN THE SAME BUILD (payload shape changed). (rule)

## LOADER REGISTRATION FIX (2026-06-12, commit 45ec6a6)
- Root cause of "mod Active but nothing runs": official loader discovers mod classes ONLY via assembly-level [assembly: RegisterModClass(typeof(ModEntry))] + a class-level scope attribute. Extending ModBigAmbitionsBase alone = "[ModDiscovery] No RegisterModClassAttribute attributes were found" and OnLoadAsync never fires. "Active" in the Mods menu only means discovered+enabled, NOT loaded. (rule)
- Scope choice: [ModEntryOnInitializationLoad] — Initialization is ModLifecycleLoader.LifetimeScope: loaded once at boot, auto-loaded before any other scope, NOT unloaded on menu↔city transitions. MainMenu/City-scoped mods are unloaded on every scene change (would tear down patches/net/UI mid-session). (rule)
- F8 status: legacy F8 floating panel was already excised 2026-06-11; F8 today is only a dev-fallback toggle. MPCanvasUI itself is the Update host for all MP ticking (saves, cash, duty, autopilot) — NOT removable. F8 keybind retirement OK after the native menu flow is re-verified on 0.11. (rule)
- Menu injection unverified on 0.11: targets MainMenuController.startView (exists — typed compile passed) + clones Button GameObject named "LoadGameButton" (scene name, unverified). [MenuUI] log lines will report on next launch. (situational: until next smoke test)

## CLOCK-FIGHT FIX (2026-06-12, commit f74011f)
- Client night↔day flicker root cause: TimeSync snap/drip vs the anti-skip watchdog (TickWorldClock) — watchdog reverted every sync write as a rogue skip. LATENT since 2026-06-10 (sessions always started clock-aligned; fresh-character mid-join with big offset finally triggered it). Fix: TimeSync sets volatile _wroteClock on its writes; watchdog consumes it and re-bases its window instead of rejecting. Watchdog's own revert writes don't set the flag (skip rejection unchanged). (rule)
- gi.Day/Hour/Minute ARE the live clock in 0.11 (GameManager advances them; TimeHelper reads them) — SetGameTime target was correct; the revert was our own watchdog, not the game. (rule)
- Character-creation on session load = CORRECT fallback for sessions whose manifest lacks the client slot (pre-TEMP-fix saves). New sessions saved after the fix should carry both slots ("2 slot(s)" in manifest log). (situational: legacy sessions from 2026-06-12 morning)

Greppable marker: "\[Audit\]". (rule)
- InteriorSync.ComputeHash now uses MPAudit.StableHash (FNV-1a) for strings instead of string.GetHashCode — REQUIRED for any hash compared across machines; GetHashCode is runtime-dependent. Rule for all future cross-machine hashes. (rule)
- Audit detection scope: synced/shared state only. NOT covered: visual-only issues (animation, model looks) and per-machine private internals — those remain eyes-on-test territory. (rule)

MPServer.Stop/MPClient.Disconnect now log Environment.StackTrace when closing live connections. NOT a mod hot-reload (single load banner). (situational: until next occurrence with forensics)
- Phantom employee at counter of replicated shop (client side, nobody hired): NOT our synthetic staff (no [SynthStaff] logs). Hypothesis: game treats replica (RentedByPlayer=false + businessOwnerRivalId=player-id + open schedule) as an AI/rival business → native staffing/simulation adopts it; possibly same root as biz price divergence. ## AI-ADOPTION SUPPRESSION (2026-06-12, commit c48ab1b)
- Phantom employee + biz-DIVERGED root cause (agent-confirmed): the game adopts every !RentedByPlayer business with NO owner-id validation — SetupAiEmployeeStations (BuildingManager, fires on building ENTER via DelayedEnterBuildingActions) spawns a fresh AI cashier per station via GetAIEmployeeInstance (no workShifts needed); CompetitionHelper.ShouldRecalculateRetailPrices re-prices daily when !RentedByPlayer+cachedAvailableProducts+allowplayercreation tag; ShouldUpdateDailyValuation mutates on any non-empty businessOwnerRivalId. Replicas of session-player shops fall through all three. (rule)
- Fix: GameStatePatcher.IsSessionPlayerBusiness(reg) (businessOwnerRivalId ∈ session players) gates three new patches: Patch_NoAiStaffInPlayerShops (prefix-skip SetupAiEmployeeStations), Patch_NoRivalRepriceOnPlayerShops, Patch_NoRivalValuationOnPlayerShops. The auditor's biz divergence was its first REAL catch — decompile corroborated. (rule)
- Employee overhaul (proposed, user asked): replace synthetic staff with the game's OWN AI-staffing path, gated by owner-reported duty — native queue/cashier/bagging via local EmployeeInstance; RemoteSale stays the revenue/stock channel; strip synthetic employees at save boundary. High plausibility (all APIs public; queue only needs a LOCAL EmployeeInstance). Personal-duty keeps self-checkout (remote avatar can't host the local Employee component without fighting position sync). (situational: pending user go-ahead)
